<b><i>Gunner, HEAT, PC!</i> Early Access Change Log</b>\r\n\r\n<color="green">(Game version: {{B}})</color>\r\n\r\nThis is a regular update introducing new content, adjustments, and fixes. As always, additional work is ongoing and will be released when ready.\r\n\r\n<color="red">DISCLAIMER:</color> GHPC is a WORK IN PROGRESS and is provided AS-IS. Many features are unfinished or unoptimized, and we ask for your patience. In addition, there may be glitches or crashes. You can help by reporting issues using the link in the "Help" section of the main menu.\r\n\r\nTo see what's in store for GHPC during Early Access, check out our development roadmap on gunnerheatpc.com! For full change log history, check the News page for GHPC on Steam.\r\n\r\n<color="green"><b>Changes from previous version:</b></color>\r\n\r\n<b>NEW CONTENT</b>\r\n\r\nAdded mission customization, allowing any completed mission to have its entire vehicle and ammunition set changed at will\r\n\r\nAdded KPz T-{{C}} UV{{D}}\r\n\r\nAdded KPz T-{{E}} UV{{F}}\r\n\r\nAdded Bradley backup {{A}}\r\nAdded M{{G}} APFSDS-T ammunition for US tanks\r\n\r\n<b>FEATURES AND ADJUSTMENTS</b>\r\n\r\nM{{H}} has been replaced by M{{I}} as the standard APFSDS ammunition for US tanks\r\n\r\nM{{J}} and M{{K}} are now both possible to find at max campaign logistics state for US forces\r\n\r\nRevised tuning of several APFSDS rounds to bring their performances more in line with expected results\r\n\r\nT-{{L}} models have been slightly revised and improved\r\n\r\nT-{{M}} tanks now have their East German names\r\n\r\nEarly model KPz T-{{N}} no longer has "Tucha" smoke grenade launchers\r\n\r\nBuffed T-{{O}} glacis armor slightly to match expected results\r\n\r\nMission result message on screen now shows the name of the mission\r\n\r\nAll planes now have pilots\r\n\r\nImproved jet trails\r\n\r\nReduced some unnecessary memory usage\r\n\r\nUpdated naming on Hind helicopters to be more precise\r\n\r\n<b>FIXES</b>\r\n\r\nFixed vegetation slider being unable to remove grass\r\n\r\nFixed an issue where tree hits would record vehicle positions for AAR, leading to some moving targets appearing to be in a different place than the main round impact and spall origin when viewing the shot in AAR mode\r\n\r\nFixed an issue where vehicles, especially trucks, could flip over at mission start\r\n\r\nFixed an issue with detecting when a percentage of enemies were eliminated, which led to some missions being difficult to complete\r\n\r\nFixed an issue with area triggers not detecting vehicles in specific situations\r\n\r\nFixed T-{{P}} front road wheels clipping the ground\r\n\r\nFixed missing night sight cover on T-{{Q}}M{{R}}\r\n\r\nFixed some visual issues on T-{{S}} and T-{{T}} models\r\n\r\nFixed some incorrectly named damage model components\r\n\r\nFixed an issue that could lead to T-{{U}}B crew treating a partial armor penetration as a full compartment incursion\r\n\r\nFixed glass textolite composite creating extra spall that could escape armor layers\r\n\r\nFixed {{V}}G{{W}} gunsight range scales moving when range setting was changed while Kobra was the selected ammunition\r\n\r\nFixed some issues with malformed vehicle number decal settings\r\n\r\nFixed an issue where T-{{X}}B flame torch effect could be detached from the vehicle\r\n\r\nFixed multiple mission layout issues\r\n\r\nFixed an issue that prevented restocking T-{{Y}} ammo racks when {{Z}}BM{{[}} was carried\r\n\r\nFixed an issue that prevented any A-{{\\}} flyovers from appearing\r\n\r\nThanks for playing!\r\n=<b><i>炮手，HEAT弹，开火！</i> 抢先体验更新日志</b>\n\n<color="green">(游戏版本: {{B}})</color>\n\n这是一次常规更新，引入了新内容、调整和修复。一如既往，额外的工作正在进行中，并将在准备就绪时发布。\n\n<color="red">免责声明:</color> GHPC是一个正在开发的作品，按现状提供。许多功能尚未完成或优化，我们请您耐心等待。此外，可能存在故障或崩溃。您可以通过主菜单"帮助"部分的链接报告问题来帮助我们。\n\n要了解GHPC在抢先体验期间的更多内容，请查看我们在gunnerheatpc.com上的开发路线图！有关完整的更新日志历史，请查看Steam上GHPC的新闻页面。\n\n<color="green"><b>与上一版本的变化:</b></color>\n\n<b>新内容</b>\n\n新增任务自定义功能，允许任何已完成的任务随意更改其整套载具和弹药配置\n\n新增KPz T-{{C}} ÜV{{D}}\n\n新增KPz T-{{E}} ÜV{{F}}\n\n新增Bradley备用{{A}}\n为美军坦克新增M{{G}} APFSDS-T弹药\n\n<b>功能和调整</b>\n\nM{{H}}已被M{{I}}替换为美军坦克的标准APFSDS弹药\n\nM{{J}}和M{{K}}现在都可以在美军最大战役后勤状态下找到\n\n修订了几种APFSDS弹药的调校，使其性能更符合预期结果\n\nT-{{L}}型号已稍作修订和改进\n\nT-{{M}}坦克现在使用其东德名称\n\n早期型KPz T-{{N}}不再配备"Tucha"烟雾榴弹发射器\n\n略微增强T-{{O}}前装甲以匹配预期结果\n\n屏幕上的任务结果消息现在显示任务名称\n\n所有飞机现在都配备飞行员\n\n改进了喷气机尾迹\n\n减少了一些不必要的内存使用\n\n更新了雌鹿直升机的命名以更加精确\n\n<b>修复</b>\n\n修复了植被滑块无法移除草地的问题\n\n修复了树木命中会记录载具位置用于AAR的问题，该问题导致在AAR模式下查看射击时，一些移动目标显示位置与主弹着点和破片起源位置不同\n\n修复了载具（特别是卡车）可能在任务开始时翻车的问题\n\n修复了检测敌军消灭百分比的问题，该问题导致一些任务难以完成\n\n修复了区域触发器在特定情况下无法检测载具的问题\n\n修复了T-{{P}}前负重轮穿透地面的问题\n\n修复了T-{{Q}}M{{R}}缺失夜视镜盖的问题\n\n修复了T-{{S}}和T-{{T}}型号的一些视觉问题\n\n修复了一些命名错误的损伤模型组件\n\n修复了可能导致T-{{U}}B乘员将部分装甲穿透视为完整车厢入侵的问题\n\n修复了玻璃纤维复合材料产生额外破片并可能逃逸装甲层的问题\n\n修复了在选择Kobra弹药时更改距离设置会导致{{V}}G{{W}}瞄准镜距离刻度移动的问题\n\n修复了一些载具编号贴花设置格式错误的问题\n\n修复了T-{{X}}B火焰喷射器效果可能与载具分离的问题\n\n修复了多个任务布局问题\n\n修复了携带{{Z}}BM{{[}}时无法补充T-{{Y}}弹药架的问题\n\n修复了任何A-{{\\}}飞越都无法出现的问题\n\n感谢游玩！\n

Hold on as long as you can until your reinforcements of tanks arrive. Once they arrive, use them to sweep the position clear of all enemies. \r\n\r\nEnd Conditions- \r\n-Blue Victory- {{P}}% Enemy Destroyed.\r\n-Blue Defeat- Loss of player tank section\r\n=态势：您的机械化排已构筑阵地，准备迎击敌军对您阵地的进攻。\n\n敌军：连级兵力，{{A}}辆BTR{{B}}，{{C}}个步兵班，以及{{D}}辆T-{{E}}\n\n友军：{{F}}辆M{{G}}，{{H}}个步兵班，以及{{I}}辆M{{J}}A{{K}}作为增援。支援资产为{{L}}次火力支援任务。\n\n任务：您需要粉碎敌军对您阵地的进攻。\n\n协调指令：您的{{M}}辆M{{N}}和{{O}}个步兵班已沿山脊线构筑阵地。在您的坦克增援抵达前，请尽可能坚守。增援抵达后，利用他们肃清阵地上的所有敌军。\n\n结束条件-\n-蓝方胜利- 摧毁{{P}}%的敌军。\n-蓝方失败- 玩家坦克分队被摧毁\n

Campaign mode is work-in-progress. The mode currently serves up a randomized selection of missions with basic mechanics determining the force compositions and victory progress.\n\n&lt;color\="yellow&gt;If you are new to GHPC, we recommend that you play the first several Instant Action missions and the gunnery training scenarios before starting a campaign. Campaign mode is not beginner-friendly.&lt;/color&gt;\n\nCampaign mode will be overhauled in the future, introducing more detail and features. You can learn more on the roadmap section of gunnerheatpc.com.=战役模式仍在开发中。该模式目前提供随机选择的任务，部队构成和胜利进程由基本机制决定。\n\n&lt;color\="yellow&gt;如果您是GHPC的新玩家，我们建议您在开始战役前，先进行前几个即时行动任务和炮术训练场景。战役模式不适合新手。&lt;/color&gt;\n\n战役模式未来将进行全面改革，引入更多细节和功能。您可以在gunnerheatpc.com的路线图部分了解更多信息。

<b><i>Gunner, HEAT, PC!</i> Early Access Change Log</b>\r\n\r\n<color="green">(Game version: {{B}})</color>\r\n\r\nThis is a minor update. As always, additional work is ongoing and will be released when ready.\r\n\r\n<color="red">DISCLAIMER:</color> GHPC is a WORK IN PROGRESS and is provided AS-IS. Many features are unfinished or unoptimized, and we ask for your patience. In addition, there may be glitches or crashes. You can help by reporting issues using the link in the "Help" section of the main menu.\r\n\r\nTo see what's in store for GHPC during Early Access, check out our development roadmap on gunnerheatpc.com! For full change log history, check the News page for GHPC on Steam.\r\n\r\n<color="green"><b>Changes from previous version:</b></color>\r\n\r\nFixed an issue that could cause vehicles, especially wheeled vehicles, to be physically unstable\r\n\r\n<color="green"><b>Changes in previous regular update:</b></color>\r\n\r\n<b>NEW CONTENT</b>\r\n\r\nAdded Marder A{{C}}+ IFV with unique "thermal pointer" night {{A}}\r\nAdded ability to switch night sight mode or polarity (default: LCtrl + T)\r\n\r\n<b>FEATURES AND ADJUSTMENTS</b>\r\n\r\nAdded manual reloading feature (default behavior can be changed in game settings)\r\n\r\nOverhauled thermal sight rendering to use more realistic resolutions and image effects\r\n\r\nImproved Marder engine sound\r\n\r\nImproved MG{{D}} exterior sound\r\n\r\nImproved consistency of audible distance and falloff effects for various gun and explosion sounds\r\n\r\nMade Marder A{{E}}+ the standard variant in missions\r\n\r\nOptimized several aspects of vehicle driving physics for performance\r\n\r\nOptimized infantry ragdoll physics for performance\r\n\r\nAuto-sorted loose vehicles in swap menu\r\n\r\n<b>FIXES</b>\r\n\r\nFixed incorrect gearing on Marder\r\n\r\nFixed armor issues on Marder hull that made it extra vulnerable to small caliber threats\r\n\r\nFixed an issue that could result in troops not posing in AAR mode\r\n\r\nFixed Bradley reticles showing as red instead of yellow in thermal {{A}}\r\nFixed incorrect infantry and helicopter crew casualty counts in mission results\r\n\r\nFixed dismounted infantry showing up as cold in thermal views\r\n\r\nFixed a squealing audio artifact on certain cannon blast sounds\r\n\r\nFixed an issue that caused {{F}}BM{{G}} ammo in racks to not respond to impacts\r\n\r\nFixed various issues that could lead to audio cutting out\r\n\r\nFixed some audio effects being noticeably too loud at distance\r\n\r\nThanks for playing!\r\n=<b><i>炮手，HEAT弹，开火！</i> 抢先体验更新日志</b>\n\n<color="green">(游戏版本: {{B}})</color>\n\n这是一次小型更新。一如既往，额外的工作正在进行中，并将在准备就绪时发布。\n\n<color="red">免责声明:</color> GHPC是一个正在进行的开发项目，按现状提供。许多功能尚未完成或优化，我们请您耐心等待。此外，可能出现故障或崩溃。您可以通过主菜单"帮助"部分的链接报告问题来帮助我们。\n\n要了解GHPC在抢先体验期间的更多内容，请查看我们在gunnerheatpc.com上的开发路线图！有关完整的更新日志历史，请查看Steam上GHPC的新闻页面。\n\n<color="green"><b>与上一版本的变化:</b></color>\n\n修复了可能导致载具（特别是轮式载具）物理不稳定的问题\n\n<color="green"><b>上一次常规更新的变化:</b></color>\n\n<b>新内容</b>\n\n新增Marder A{{C}}+ 步兵战车，配备独特的"热成像指示器"夜视{{A}}\n新增切换夜视镜模式或极性的功能（默认: LCtrl + T）\n\n<b>功能和调整</b>\n\n新增手动装填功能（默认行为可在游戏设置中更改）\n\n全面改进热成像瞄准镜渲染，使用更逼真的分辨率和图像效果\n\n改进了Marder发动机声音\n\n改进了MG{{D}}外部声音\n\n改进了各种火炮和爆炸声音的可听距离和衰减效果的一致性\n\n将Marder A{{E}}+ 设为任务中的标准变体\n\n优化了载具驾驶物理的多个方面以提升性能\n\n优化了步兵布娃娃物理以提升性能\n\n自动排序载具切换菜单中的散装载具\n\n<b>修复</b>\n\n修复了Marder档位不正确的问题\n\n修复了Marder车体装甲问题，该问题使其对小口径威胁特别脆弱\n\n修复了可能导致部队在AAR模式下无法摆姿势的问题\n\n修复了Bradley瞄准具在热成像{{A}}中显示为红色而非黄色的问题\n修复了任务结果中步兵和直升机机组人员伤亡统计错误的问题\n\n修复了下车步兵在热成像视图中显示为冷目标的问题\n\n修复了某些火炮爆炸声音中的尖啸音频问题\n\n修复了导致弹药架中{{F}}BM{{G}}弹药无法响应撞击的问题\n\n修复了可能导致音频中断的各种问题\n\n修复了某些音效在远距离时声音明显过大的问题\n\n感谢游玩！\n

Support assets are {{J}}x HE, and {{K}}x Smoke fire missions.\r\n\r\nMission: You are to move to friendly locations that are attacked by the enemy and support them.\r\n\r\nEnd Conditions- \r\n-Blue Victory- Destroy all enemy attacks\r\n-Blue Defeat- Loss of player IFV platoon, or loss of friendly infantry.\r\n=态势: 敌军正在对我方防线发起一系列机械化攻击。\n\n敌军: 连级兵力，BTR{{A}}，BMP{{B}}，BMP{{C}}，和T{{D}}\n\n友军: {{E}}辆Marder A{{F}}+，{{G}}辆M{{H}}G，{{I}}个步兵班。支援资源包括{{J}}次HE火力支援和{{K}}次烟幕火力任务。\n\n任务: 您需要前往遭到敌军攻击的友军位置并支援他们。\n\n结束条件- \n-蓝方胜利- 摧毁所有敌军攻击\n-蓝方失败- 玩家步兵战车排全损，或友军步兵全损。\n

Situation: Your company is tasked with setting up hasty defensive positions along a major road behind an American heavy cavalry squadron. They have been engaged with an NVA regiment for the last {{A}} hours and have been withdrawing through your position for the last half hour. The Americans report the enemy is attempting to attack down the flanks of the road instead of directly down it. We expect the last of the Americans within {{B}} minutes and the enemy to be right behind them. We also expect the rest of our battalion to reinforce us in {{C}} hours.\r\n\r\nEnemy: Company Strength, {{D}}x T{{E}}A, {{F}}x BTR{{G}}, {{H}}x infantry squads.\r\n\r\nFriendly: {{I}}x Leo A{{J}}A{{K}}, {{L}}x M{{M}}G, {{N}}x Infantry squads. Reinforcements of {{O}}x Leo A{{P}}A{{Q}}. Support assets are {{R}}x fire missions,and {{S}}x WP Smoke missions.\r\n\r\nMission: With your {{T}} tanks, you are to cover {{U}}rd mech platoon as they finish digging in at Battle Position (BP) Alpha. If forced to withdraw, you are to move to where you are needed.\r\n\r\nCoordinating instructions: {{V}}rd mech is finishing digging in half its force at BP Alpha, they will send the other half back to BP Bravo to dig in there. {{W}}th Mech platoon is digging in at BP Delta with a light scout force out at BP Charlie. We expect our {{X}}nd tank platoon to arrive in {{Y}} minutes \r\n\r\nEnd Conditions-\r\n-Blue Victory- {{Z}}% enemies destroyed\r\n-Blue Defeat- Loss of all player tanks\r\n=态势: 您的连队奉命在一条主要道路沿线建立仓促防御阵地，位于一个美军重装骑兵中队后方。他们与人民军一个团交战已达{{A}}小时，过去半小时一直在通过您的阵地撤退。美军报告敌军试图从道路两侧发起攻击，而非直接沿路攻击。我们预计最后一批美军将在{{B}}分钟内通过，敌军紧随其后。我们还预计营部其余部队将在{{C}}小时内增援我们。\n\n敌军: 连级兵力，{{D}}辆T{{E}}A，{{F}}辆BTR{{G}}，{{H}}个步兵班。\n\n友军: {{I}}辆Leo A{{J}}A{{K}}，{{L}}辆M{{M}}G，{{N}}个步兵班。增援部队{{O}}辆Leo A{{P}}A{{Q}}。支援资源包括{{R}}次火力支援任务和{{S}}次WP烟幕任务。\n\n任务: 使用您的{{T}}辆坦克，掩护第{{U}}机械化排在战斗阵地(BP) Alpha完成构筑工事。如被迫撤退，应前往需要您的地点。\n\n协调指令: 第{{V}}机械化排正在BP Alpha完成半数兵力的构筑工事，他们将派遣另一半返回BP Bravo在那里构筑工事。第{{W}}机械化排正在BP Delta构筑工事，并在BP Charlie派出轻型侦察兵力。我们预计第{{X}}坦克排将在{{Y}}分钟内到达\n\n结束条件-\n-蓝方胜利- 消灭{{Z}}%敌军\n-蓝方失败- 玩家坦克全损\n

As always, additional work is ongoing and will be released when ready.\r\n\r\n<color="red">DISCLAIMER:</color> GHPC is a WORK IN PROGRESS and is provided AS-IS. Many features are unfinished or unoptimized, and we ask for your patience. In addition, there may be glitches or crashes. You can help by reporting issues using the link in the "Help" section of the main menu.\r\n\r\nTo see what's in store for GHPC during Early Access, check out our development roadmap on gunnerheatpc.com! For full change log history, check the News page for GHPC on Steam.\r\n\r\n<color="green"><b>Changes from previous version:</b></color>\r\n\r\nFixed the M{{C}}A{{D}} (non-TTS) having no usable night vision mode\r\n\r\nFixed an issue that would vertically invert the entire gunsight view in the Marder night sight on certain graphics API setups\r\n\r\n\r\n<color="green"><b>Changes in previous regular update:</b></color>\r\n\r\n<b>NEW CONTENT</b>\r\n\r\nAdded Marder A{{E}}+ IFV with unique "thermal pointer" night {{A}}\r\nAdded ability to switch night sight mode or polarity (default: LCtrl + T)\r\n\r\n<b>FEATURES AND ADJUSTMENTS</b>\r\n\r\nAdded manual reloading feature (default behavior can be changed in game settings)\r\n\r\nOverhauled thermal sight rendering to use more realistic resolutions and image effects\r\n\r\nImproved Marder engine sound\r\n\r\nImproved MG{{F}} exterior sound\r\n\r\nImproved consistency of audible distance and falloff effects for various gun and explosion sounds\r\n\r\nMade Marder A{{G}}+ the standard variant in missions\r\n\r\nOptimized several aspects of vehicle driving physics for performance\r\n\r\nOptimized infantry ragdoll physics for performance\r\n\r\nAuto-sorted loose vehicles in swap menu\r\n\r\n<b>FIXES</b>\r\n\r\nFixed incorrect gearing on Marder\r\n\r\nFixed armor issues on Marder hull that made it extra vulnerable to small caliber threats\r\n\r\nFixed an issue that could result in troops not posing in AAR mode\r\n\r\nFixed Bradley reticles showing as red instead of yellow in thermal {{A}}\r\nFixed incorrect infantry and helicopter crew casualty counts in mission results\r\n\r\nFixed dismounted infantry showing up as cold in thermal views\r\n\r\nFixed a squealing audio artifact on certain cannon blast sounds\r\n\r\nFixed an issue that caused {{H}}BM{{I}} ammo in racks to not respond to impacts\r\n\r\nFixed various issues that could lead to audio cutting out\r\n\r\nFixed some audio effects being noticeably too loud at distance\r\n\r\nThanks for playing!\r\n=<b><i>炮手，HEAT弹，开火！</i> 抢先体验更新日志</b>\r\n\r\n<color="green">(游戏版本: Map: Point Alpha\nYour platoon's mission is to destroy enemy screening forces before they can give a report on your position. You are then to disrupt enemy forces on TGT{{A}}.  Our recon has spotted an enemy armor company of {{B}} vehicles forming for an attack there. Recon reports the screening forces are likely APCs. The pre-planned artillery is waiting on your initiation of contact with the main enemy force. The attack will be a success if you destroy even a small number of vehicles from this attack force. It will be a loss if you lose more than half your force.\n\n\nDue to communication disruptions and recon unit losses, intelligence on the composition of the enemy threat is unavailable.\r\n\r\nFriendly forces (German National People's Army):\r\n\r\nTank - T-{{C}}A\n\r\n\r\nEnemy forces (US Army):\r\n\r\nUNKNOWN\r\n\r\n\r\nOther: \n\r\nOur forces are well reinforced and our first line units are fully intact.\n\r\nIntel suggests enemy forces are showing little sign of wavering.\n\r\nCurrent streak: {{D}}\r\nBest streak: {{E}}\r\n=地图：阿尔法点\n您排的任务是在敌方掩护部队报告您的位置之前将其摧毁。然后您要袭扰目标{{A}}上的敌军。我们的侦察发现敌方一个由{{B}}辆载具组成的装甲连正在那里准备攻击。侦察报告掩护部队可能是APC。预先规划的火炮正在等待您与敌方主力接触。如果您能摧毁该攻击部队的哪怕少量载具，攻击就算成功。如果您损失超过一半兵力，则为失败。\n\n\n由于通信中断和侦察单位损失，无法获得敌方威胁构成的情报。\r\n\r\n友军（德国国家人民军）：\r\n\r\n坦克 - T-{{C}}A\n\r\n\r\n敌军（美军）：\r\n\r\n未知\r\n\r\n\r\n其他：\n\r\n我们的部队得到良好增援，一线部队完好无损。\n\r\n情报显示敌军几乎没有动摇迹象。\n\r\n当前连胜：{{D}}\r\n最佳连胜：{{E}}\r\n

Situation: You stopped the enemy's attack approximately {{A}} hours ago. The rest of your battalion has arrived and is planning a limited counter-attack. Our scouts have observed the enemy is in the process of digging in and an attack any later in the future would be more difficult. Friendly divisional artillery is conducting counter battery fire missions to suppress the enemy's access to artillery for this attack.\r\n\r\nEnemy: Company Strength, {{B}}x T{{C}}A, {{D}}x BTR{{E}}, {{F}}x infantry squads. {{G}}x T{{H}} reserve force\r\n\r\nFriendly: {{I}}x Leo A{{J}}A{{K}}, {{L}}x M{{M}}G, {{N}}x Infantry squads. Reinforcements of {{O}}x Leo A{{P}}A{{Q}}. Support assets are {{R}}x fire missions,and {{S}}x WP Smoke missions.\r\n\r\nMission: With your {{T}} tanks, you engage enemy forces on OBJ Cougar in order to support {{U}}rd mech platoon's dismounted infantry attack on it. Once OBJ Cougar is taken, {{V}}nd tank and {{W}}th mech will move up to support you. You will then move to engage any enemy forces on OBJ Ocelot to support {{X}}th platoon's dismounted infantry attack on it.\r\n\r\nCoordinating instructions: Your infantry will attack once you have engaged the enemy on OBJ Cougar. Your infantry will attack OBJ Ocelot once you have destroyed the enemy armor on OBJ Ocelot.\r\n\r\nEnd Conditions-\r\n-Blue Victory- {{Y}}% Enemy Destroyed and Objectives Cougar & Ocelot taken.\r\n-Blue Defeat- Loss of all player tanks\r\n=态势：您在大约{{A}}小时前阻止了敌军的攻击。您的营其余部队已经抵达，正在计划有限的反击。我方侦察兵观察到敌军正在构筑工事，如果再拖延攻击将更加困难。友军师属炮兵正在执行反炮兵火力任务，以压制敌军在此次攻击中的炮兵支援。\r\n\r\n敌军：连级力量，{{B}}辆T{{C}}A，{{D}}辆BTR{{E}}，{{F}}个步兵班。{{G}}辆T{{H}}预备部队\r\n\r\n友军：{{I}}辆Leo A{{J}}A{{K}}，{{L}}辆M{{M}}G，{{N}}个步兵班。增援部队{{O}}辆Leo A{{P}}A{{Q}}。支援火力为{{R}}次火力任务和{{S}}次WP烟幕任务。\r\n\r\n任务：使用您的{{T}}辆坦克，攻击目标美洲狮上的敌军，以支援第{{U}}机械化排的下车步兵攻击。一旦夺取目标美洲狮，第{{V}}坦克排和第{{W}}机械化排将前出支援您。然后您将前进攻击目标豹猫上的任何敌军，以支援第{{X}}排的下车步兵攻击。\r\n\r\n协调指令：一旦您与目标美洲狮上的敌军交战，您的步兵将发起攻击。一旦您摧毁目标豹猫上的敌方装甲，您的步兵将攻击目标豹猫。\r\n\r\n结束条件-\r\n-蓝方胜利-{{Y}}%敌军被摧毁且目标美洲狮和豹猫被夺取。\r\n-蓝方失败-所有玩家坦克损失\r\n
This is a simple mission to get used to the Leopard A{{A}}A{{B}} and its fire control. There will be {{C}} targets total: four of them static and {{D}} of them moving, all of them at different ranges.\r\n\r\n-A quick guide to using the fire control system\r\nPress Shift to enter the gunsight. Hold the right mouse button to move the gun. Center the gunsight on the target. Press E to enable the stereoscopic rangefinder. Press CTRL+Mouse Wheel (or PgUp and PgDown) and adjust the range until the target comes into focus. This will range your gun to the correct distance. Press E and use your normal gunsight to engage the enemy. Repeat these steps to kill all targets.\r\n\r\n-If you press C when looking through your gunsight, it will switch to your backup sight.\r\n-The night sight does not have the stereoscopic rangefinder.\r\n-The HUD shows your current range setting. Make sure you’re using a range that makes sense for the current target, especially if the coincidence rangefinder isn’t clear enough.\r\n\r\n-Simple Leopard A{{E}}A{{F}} ammunition description\r\nAPDS is a dart that flies fast and is good at killing tanks.\r\nHEAT is an explosive that flies slow and is good for killing vehicles lighter than tanks, as well as old tanks.\r\nHESH is an explosive that flies slow and is good for killing vehicles lighter than tanks, as well as old tanks.\r\n\r\nYou can see this briefing in the mission if you press M on your keyboard.\r\n=本任务旨在帮助您熟悉Leopard A{{A}}A{{B}}及其火控系统。总计有{{C}}个目标：4个固定目标和{{D}}个移动目标，均处于不同距离。\r\n\r\n-火控系统快速使用指南\r\n按Shift键进入炮手瞄准镜。按住鼠标右键移动火炮。将瞄准镜中心对准目标。按E键启用体视测距仪。按CTRL+鼠标滚轮（或PgUp和PgDown键）调整测距，直到目标图像清晰重合。这将为您的火炮标定正确距离。再按E键切换回主瞄准镜与敌交战。重复以上步骤，消灭所有目标。\r\n\r\n-在炮手瞄准镜视角下按C键，将切换至备用瞄准镜。\r\n-夜视瞄准镜没有体视测距功能。\r\n-抬头显示器（HUD）会显示您当前的测距设定。请确保该距离与当前目标相符，尤其是在合像式测距仪图像不够清晰时。\r\n\r\n-Leopard A{{E}}A{{F}}弹药简介\r\nAPDS是一种高速飞行的穿甲弹，擅于摧毁坦克。\r\nHEAT是一种低速飞行的爆炸物，适用于摧毁轻于坦克的载具及旧式坦克。\r\nHESH是一种低速飞行的爆炸物，适用于摧毁轻于坦克的载具及旧式坦克。\r\n\r\n任务期间，您可以随时按M键查看此简报。\r\n

This is a simple mission to get used to the Marder A{{A}}+ and its fire control. There will be {{B}} targets total: four of them static and {{C}} of them moving, all of them at different ranges.\r\n\r\n-A quick guide to using the fire control system\r\nPress Shift to enter the gunsight. Hold the right mouse button to move the gun. Press CTRL+Mouse Wheel (or PgUp and PgDown) to range the gun using the range number in the HUD. Center the gunsight on the target, and aim ahead of the target’s position if the target is moving. Fire on the target and adjust your range as needed. Repeat these steps to kill all targets.\r\n\r\nTo use the nightsight press T when looking through the gunsight. Then press N to turn on the IR searchlight. On the Marder A{{D}}+ version you can press left CTRL + T to turn on the thermal overlay.\r\n\r\n-The Milan missile is used if you press F to switch to it. Hold the left mouse button to fire, and keep the reticle centered on your target to kill it. The missile launcher has no nightsight.\r\n\r\n-Simple Marder A{{E}}+ ammunition description\r\nAPI-T is a slug that is good at killing APCs and IFVs\r\nHE is an explosive that is good for killing infantry and trucks.\r\nMilan is a missile that is good at killing tanks.\r\n=本任务旨在帮助您熟悉Marder A{{A}}+及其火控系统。总计有{{B}}个目标：4个固定目标和{{C}}个移动目标，均处于不同距离。\r\n\r\n-火控系统快速使用指南\r\n按Shift键进入炮手瞄准镜。按住鼠标右键移动火炮。按CTRL+鼠标滚轮（或PgUp和PgDown键）依据抬头显示器（HUD）上的距离数据进行测距。将瞄准镜中心对准目标，若目标正在移动，需进行提前量瞄准。向目标开火，并根据需要调整测距。重复以上步骤，消灭所有目标。\r\n\r\n在炮手瞄准镜视角下按T键使用夜视瞄准镜。然后按N键开启红外探照灯。在Marder A{{D}}+型号上，您可以按左CTRL+T键开启热成像。\r\n\r\n-按F键可切换至Milan导弹。按住鼠标左键发射，并保持瞄准线持续对准目标直至命中。导弹发射器无夜视功能。\r\n\r\n-Marder A{{E}}+弹药简介\r\nAPI-T是一种穿甲弹，擅于摧毁APC和IFV。\r\nHE是一种高爆弹，适用于消灭步兵和卡车。\r\nMilan是一种导弹，擅于摧毁坦克。\r\n

Our scouts have observed the enemy is in the process of digging in and an attack any later in the future would be more difficult. Once OBJ Cougar is taken, {{V}}nd tank and {{W}}th mech will move up to support you. You will then move to engage any enemy forces on OBJ Ocelot to support {{X}}th platoon’s dismounted infantry attack on it.\r\n\r\nCoordinating instructions: Your infantry will attack once you have engaged the enemy on OBJ Cougar. Your infantry will attack OBJ Ocelot once you have destroyed the enemy armor on OBJ Ocelot.\r\n\r\nEnd Conditions-\r\n-Blue Victory- {{Y}}% Enemy Destroyed and Objectives Cougar &amp; Ocelot taken.\r\n-Blue Defeat- Loss of all player tanks\r\n=态势: 您在大约{{A}}小时前阻止了敌军攻击。营其余部队已抵达，正在计划有限反击。我方侦察兵观察到敌军正在挖掘工事，未来任何延迟攻击都将更困难。友军师级炮兵正在执行反炮兵火力任务，以压制敌军在本攻击中的炮兵使用。\r\n\r\n敌军: 连级规模，{{B}}辆T{{C}}A，{{D}}辆BTR{{E}}，{{F}}个步兵班。{{G}}辆T{{H}}预备力量\r\n\r\n友军: {{I}}辆Leo A{{J}}A{{K}}，{{L}}辆M{{M}}G，{{N}}个步兵班。增援部队{{O}}辆Leo A{{P}}A{{Q}}。支援资产包括{{R}}次火力任务，以及{{S}}次WP烟幕任务。\r\n\r\n任务: 使用您的{{T}}辆坦克，交战目标Cougar上的敌军力量，以支援{{U}}机械化排的下车步兵对其攻击。一旦目标Cougar被占领，{{V}}坦克和{{W}}机械化部队将上前支援您。然后您将移动交战目标Ocelot上的任何敌军力量，以支援{{X}}排的下车步兵对其攻击。\r\n\r\n协调指令: 一旦您交战目标Cougar上的敌军，您的步兵将发起攻击。一旦您摧毁目标Ocelot上的敌军装甲，您的步兵将攻击目标Ocelot。\r\n\r\n结束条件-\r\n-蓝方胜利- {{Y}}%敌军被摧毁且目标Cougar &amp; Ocelot被占领。\r\n-蓝方失败- 损失所有玩家坦克

regular update:</b></color>\r\n\r\n<b>NEW CONTENT</b>\r\n\r\nAdded Marder A{{D}}+ IFV with unique "thermal pointer" night sight\r\n\r\nAdded ability to switch night sight mode or polarity (default: LCtrl + T)\r\n\r\n<b>FEATURES AND ADJUSTMENTS</b>\r\n\r\nAdded manual reloading feature (default behavior can be changed in game settings)\r\n\r\nOverhauled thermal sight rendering to use more
